For example, in the URL "https://fortune.com/2024/11/04/harris-trump-victory-the-markets-unless-winner-sweeps-congress/", "https" is the protocol used, which is a secure version of HTTP. 

It's worth noting that HTTP is not the only protocol used in web addresses. Other protocols, such as FTP (File Transfer Protocol), can also be used, depending on the purpose of the website or the type of data being transferred. However, HTTP remains the most widely used protocol for web browsing.
